(enchant:?page,(text-colour:black)) (text-style:"shadow")+(text-style:"fade-in-out")[''A Metamorphosing''] (b4r:"groove")+(b4r-colour:purple)+(text-style:"condense")[//"The butterfly does not look back upon its caterpillar self, either fondly or wistfully. It simply flies on."// //The Night Eternal, Guillermo del Toro.//] [^^//Note to Reader// The chapters are arranged on the main page in the chronological order. As you click through the chapters, you will see some chapters do not lead you to the next chronological chapter. You can follow the path or come back to the main page to read in the order here. It's for you to connect the dots and enjoy as you like.^^] [[Hole in the wall]] [[The Rebel is dead]] [[The Caterpillar]] [[Ecological Genetics]] [[Silence and Emptiness]] [[DNA]] [[Adaptation / Learnings]] [[The Chrysalis]] [[I don't know where the house ends and I begin.]] [[Eco-Evo-Devo]] [[Darwinism]] [[Metamorphosis]] [[The Night Eternal]] ^^[[about the author]]^^(enchant:?page,(text-colour:black)) (text-color:blue)+(text-style:"outline")[I want to talk to you about the hole in my wall.] ^^Well not necessarily in the wall, but it’s on a digital print on my kitchen’s wall that I hanged when I first moved into my new apartment. I bought that digital print in January 2021. The artist was in the very first exhibition I curated, and the work is a part of her series called Radical Expression. In this print, she played with the words (text-colour:green)[//Fitting in//] and the (text-color:red)[//Rebellious one//] with some shapes overlapping and demonstrating the functionality of the words. I always thought of myself as unconventional, (text-color:red)[//rebellious one//], who always stayed true to what she believed in. Thus, the print was a part of my identity. It is very relatable. I loved it.^^ ^^In May 2021, that very same words started to bother me. House raids were common during those times. If you are unlucky, any item is a suspicious item, and you get arrested. So, I took that 70$ print off the wall, lay out all my tools on the table, cut out the word (text-color:red)[//Rebellious one//] from the print and burned it. I didn’t need to burn it, but I thought I would do a little send-off ritual. For the little piece of cut out paper and for a part of myself that does not exist anymore. I didn’t want them to think I had something to do with (text-color:red)[//the rebels//], as they have named the protestors and armed insurgencies who work against them.^^ [[Hole in the wall]] [[Silence and Emptiness]] [[I don't know where the house ends and I begin.]] [[Main Page ->A Metamorphosing]] (enchant:?page,(text-colour:black)) ''The Caterpillar'' //the larva stage of a butterfly or moth. A small worm like animals that feeds on plants// ^^Empathy is the best communicator of human experiences. Without empathy, stories are just information, history just facts. Empathy connects us, binds us with one another. It helps us feel, understand, and vividly experience another person’s encounters through their recount.I was not empathic when it comes to Myanmar’s past. The (his)tories of Myanmar’s democratic struggles enticed me, but I never really related to it. The violence was foreign; so was the determinations, the hate, the struggles, the sacrifices. The black and white photos looked so old, and the repeated recalls of the struggles bored me. (text-style:"sway")[What was the point?]^^ ^^My definition of self was detached from the pain of my ancestors. The burdens of the past, I did not want to carry. I did not want to recount. I was going to be the one to (text-style:"smear")[escape]. I wanted to cut all the ties.^^ [[The Chrysalis]] [[Main Page ->A Metamorphosing]] (enchant:?page,(text-colour:black)) ''Ecological Genetics'' //study of evolutionary processes, especially adaptation by natural selection// ^^If I am lucky enough to live for many more years, and someone ask me what I remember about the Coup, I would just vividly recall the silent road I see from my apartment windows at night. Me and my mother invested in a very well-lit apartment in a very busy neighborhood back in January 2021. Convenience was one of the great things about this place, the stores, the nearby market, the cafés, the restaurants. With all these spots nearby, the surrounding is very lively. One of the concerns I had about this place was the traffic noise. Yangon has become quite a lively city in the recent years. People go out till dark into the night and the cars never left the streets. For me, it’s the sign of a prospering city, of people feeling alive. The anticipated concern was not necessary, needless to say, as the enforced curfew time nowadays is from 10 pm to 4 am. People usually stop going out around 8 pm. It’s very easy to get shot in the dark or be mistaken for underground armed groups. The silence is uncomfortable and very uncanny. (text-style:"condense")[With silence, there is emptiness. In the silence and in the emptiness is (text-style:"rumble")[fear], (text-style:"fade-in-out")[the knowing of what’s in the dark.]] The (text-color:green)+(text-style:"condense")[goblins] from the stories are (text-color:green)+(text-style:"condense")[green], and they carry (text-color:red)+(text-style:"condense")[fireworks]. They are watching you. They will come for you.^^ [[Image ->Silence and Emptiness]] [[Adaptation / Learnings]] [[Main Page ->A Metamorphosing]] (text-color:grey)[''Silence and Emptiness''] <img [[The Chrysalis]] [[The Rebel is dead]] [[Silence and Emptiness]] [[Main Page ->A Metamorphosing]] (enchant:?page,(text-colour:black)) (text-color:red)[''DNA''] //carrier of genetic info. A self-replicating material// //the fundamental and distinctive characteristics or qualities of someone or something, especially when regarded as unchangeable// ^^For those who knows how this regime works, it’s going back to the familiar. (text-style:"strike")[Exiled, censored, blacklisted, arrested, underground], they are all too familiar with these words. Immediate response system and old routines of working under Dictatorship kicked in as if it’s in their (text-color:red)[blood]. Those like me, who are on the younger side, wasn’t lost on what to do either. After 70 years of conflicts and 3 bloody coups, it’s like (text-colour:red)[DNA], a passed down tradition, a heritage of knowledge on how to survive. Through stories we have heard, horrors we have seen through a screen, we knew what was coming. (text-colour:magenta)+(text-style:"smear")[Heredity] is not empathy. (text-colour:magenta)+(text-style:"smear")[Heredity] is in the (text-color:red)[blood]. It’s a relation. It’s sacred knowledge passed down from generations to generations, information gathered by your ancestors through their whole life experiences on how to survive your predators. They are survival tactics, mechanisms of resilience, an instinctive knowing, and your brain signaling to fight or flight. [[Empathy ->The Caterpillar]] can never teach you that.^^ [[Ecological Genetics]] [[Main Page ->A Metamorphosing]] (enchant:?page,(text-colour:black)) (text-style:"smear")+(text-colour:orange)[''Adaptation / Learnings''] ^^(text-style:"blur")[What is the difference between the sound of a sound bomb and a gunfire?] (text-style:"blur")[How do you differentiate the sound of rubber bullets and actual bullets?] (text-style:"blur")[How do you create a smokescreen so that the snipers cannot aim for you?] (text-style:"blur")[How do you defend against the smoke bombs?] My 16 years old younger cousin came to visit my new apartment when I finally moved in in April. She looked at the letter opener knife on my desk and said, (text-style:"shudder")[**“That looks like a sharp object. Maybe you should keep it hidden or have an excuse ready if they raid your place.”**]^^ [[Ecological Genetics]] [[Eco-Evo-Devo]] [[Darwinism]] [[Main Page ->A Metamorphosing]] (enchant:?page,(text-colour:black)) (text-colour:magenta)+(background:(gradient: 0, 0,#ffffff,0.4967,#19e5e6,1,#ffffff))[''The Chrysalis''] (text-style:"buoy")[//a butterfly or moth at the stage of development when it is covered by a hard case before it becomes an adult insect with wings or the case itself//] ^^I rarely step out of my apartment since the coup. Sometimes, [[I don't know where the house ends and I begin.]] When July came and covid third wave hits Myanmar, I was trapped in the apartment for about 2 months. You don’t necessarily need to step out of the house to know what’s happening. The images on social media of long lines at the crematoriums, the lack of oxygen, the panic, the heartbreak, and powerlessness of having to watch your loved ones die in front of you are not hard to believe with ambulance noises echoing through the neighborhood the whole day. As I watch the (text-style:"blink")+(text-color:red)[blinking red lights] through my window, the apartment became my cocoon. I wondered what is the formula that is being brewed in (text-colour:magenta)+(background:(gradient: 0, 0,#ffffff,0.4967,#19e5e6,1,#ffffff))[this chrysalis]. The old genes and the freshly self-experienced ones could mix well together to form a new set of genetics. (text-style:"condense")[What does the new “us” look like?]^^ [[Ecological Genetics]] [[DNA]] [[Main Page ->A Metamorphosing]] (enchant:?page,(text-colour:black)) ''Eco-Evo-Devo'' //integration of research from developmental biology and ecology into evolutionary theory. Ecological Evolutionary Developmental Biology or Eco-Evo-Devo// ^^(text-style:"fade-in-out")[FUN FACTS] (text-style:"smear")+(text-colour:cyan)[Escapism] is a sweet lord. I occasionally post sob stories on my social media, and then put in a side note (text-style:"shudder")[**“Don’t come and tell me I will be okay,”**] just to sound a bit dramatic. I like the attention. (text-style:"fidget")+(text-style:"double-strike")[Min Aung Hlaing] is my show monkey. I wrote “My country is in a coup. I am suffering” to many applications from many places and so far, they love me. (b4r:"dotted")+(b4r-colour:purple)[Resilience is my father and mother.] Some mornings I don’t want to be resilient, so I curled up in my bed and sleep all day. **Be political only or you don’t matter.** Cry for the camera. Any camera. (text-colour:orange)+(background:(gradient: 0, 0,#ffffff,0.4967,#e5e619,1,#ffffff))[**The ones on the other side wants to save you.**] Their purpose on earth is to save you. Do you know (text-style:"buoy")[butterflies’s](text-colour:magenta)+(text-style:"smear")[heredity] change according to the environment they are in to protect themselves from (text-color:green)[predators] as the species evolve?^^ [[Darwinism]] [[Main Page ->A Metamorphosing]] (enchant:?page,(text-colour:black)) ''Darwinism'' //the theory of evolution of species by natural selection// //Darwinian : a competitive environment or situation in which only the (text-style:"rumble")[fittest] person or organization prospers.// ^^Natural selection is an adopted tactic for best survival. It’s the (text-style:"rumble")[survival of the fittest]. Who is considered the (text-style:"rumble")[fittest]? How can you be the (text-style:"rumble")[fittest]? Who do you align with to become the (text-style:"rumble")[fittest]? What are the rules to becoming the (text-style:"rumble")[fittest]? The (text-style:"rumble")[fittest] are perhaps (text-color:green)[green], but the best way to ensure your survival is to be a (text-color:cyan)[chameleon]. Different situations call for different colors, different masks, different standpoints. If dying is injustice, so is surviving. The Darwinian world order does not promote justice. The (text-style:"rumble")[fittest] do not care about justice. They just survive.^^ [[Ecological Genetics]] [[DNA]] [[Eco-Evo-Devo]] [[Metamorphosis]] [[Main Page ->A Metamorphosing]] <img src=https://media2.giphy.com/media/GLB3wBBarVd4Vj86RH/giphy.gif?cid=790b7611900c87b89afafd9dc79da8a7509e417ecbfe273c&rid=giphy.gif&ct=g> ^^Womb^^ (enchant:?page,(text-colour:black)) (b4r:"groove")+(b4r-size:2)+(b4r-colour:magenta) [''Metamorphosis'' //the process through which some animals abruptly transform their bodies after birth//] [[Continue ->Metamorphosis 1]] [[Main Page ->A Metamorphosing]] (b4r:"groove")+(b4r-colour:purple)+(text-colour:black)+(text-style:"condense")[//"The butterfly does not look back upon its caterpillar self, either fondly or wistfully. It simply flies on."// //The Night Eternal, Guillermo del Toro.//] (link: "click here")[(goto-url: 'https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Night_Eternal')] [[Main Page ->A Metamorphosing]] ^^[[about the author]]^^ (enchant:?page,(text-colour:black)) (b4r:"groove")+(b4r-size:2)+(b4r-colour:magenta) [^^Metamorphosis is not as pretty as mainstream perspective would make it out to be. It’s a grimy, brutal process with pre-determined genetics making up who you are. The caterpillar did not just transform into a butterfly it wants to be. Under the skin layer, is a set of dormant wings hidden since birth, ready to develop into a full adult as it goes through the pupa stage. DNA from the mother remains the same.^^] [[Continue -> Metamorphosis 3]] [[Back ->Metamorphosis]] [[Main Page ->A Metamorphosing]] (enchant:?page,(text-colour:black)) (b4r:"groove")+(b4r-size:2)+(b4r-colour:magenta) [^^Motherhood terrifies me. My womb is a kiln where I will produce more like me who couldn’t escape the fate. What will I be handing over to my successors? My genes terrify me. My history terrifies me. I cannot escape, and neither can the ones after me. Heredity cannot be changed. The knowings cannot be unlearned. My awakened genes would haunt me for a long time.^^] [[The Night Eternal]] [[Back ->Metamorphosis 2]] [[Main Page ->A Metamorphosing]] <img src="https://i.ibb.co/S6xsb0K/Metamorphosing-1.jpg" alt="Metamorphosing-1" border="0"> ^^Madam Chrysalis^^ (enchant:?page,(text-colour:black)) //**A Metamorphosing from Myanmar**// She is currently in a cocoon. She is transmuting. She is busy. But sometimes she sleeps a lot. ^^Image Credit The images Womb and Madam Chrysalis are artist Zune Htet's interpretive illustrations of the essay.^^ [[Main Page ->A Metamorphosing]](enchant:?page,(text-colour:black)) (b4r:"groove")+(b4r-size:2)+(b4r-colour:magenta) [^^On January 31st, I slept at 4 am. I worked till late night. When I finally went to bed, I noticed the telecommunications cut off and internet blackout. I put two and two together from what’s been happening in the last two days, but I ignored my instinct. Perhaps, a part of me already knew but didn’t want it to be true. Morning at 8 am, I woke up to the news of the coup.^^ ^^In the coming months of escalated horrors, the coup, the deadly covid third wave, my freedom taken away, and the (self) confinement, I was abruptly transformed into something new. As I slowly step out of my chrysalis, the patterns are formed. The trauma heritage on my body, violence heritage from ancestors, the awakened survival instincts, all of them make me wonder where this process of rebirth is heading to. What will I become? ^^] [[Continue ->Metamorphosis 2]] [[Main Page ->A Metamorphosing]]
